# Unreached GL/MIXED/AI Functions

Functions with category GL, MIXED, or AI that are **not reachable** from any of the 7 call graph trees
(game_loop, turn_pipeline, player_input, network, ai, dialogs, game_setup) at max_depth=8.

## Summary

| Metric | Count |
|--------|-------|
| Total reachable from all 7 trees | 2117 |
| Total GL/MIXED/AI in codebase | 739 |
| **Unreached GL/MIXED/AI** | **144** |
| Unreached GL | 82 |
| Unreached MIXED | 61 |
| Unreached AI | 1 |
| Functional groups | 19 |

## Scenario Editor & Cheats (25 functions)

### `00415307` copy_editor_data_to_tech

- **Category:** GL | **Size:** 275 bytes | **Importance:** editor/debug
- **Summary:** Copies technology data back from the editor buffer to the game tech table for all 100 technologies.
- **Mutations:** DAT_0062768X array written — these are in 0x0062 range (tech prerequisite/flag arrays, framework data not game state per the instructions)

**Called by:**
- `00415A40` show_messagebox_5A40 [UI] — ✗ unreached

**Calls (depth 3):**
```
copy_editor_data_to_tech
└── get_improvement_name [FW]
```

### `004A3426` save_editor_to_rules

- **Category:** GL | **Size:** 538 bytes | **Importance:** editor/debug
- **Summary:** Copies scenario editor values back into the game's rule tables. Reverse of load_rules_to_editor.
- **Mutations:** Writes to multiple game state arrays:
- DAT_0064bcf8 (0x0064 range — leader data per civ)
- DAT_00655500, DAT_006554f8-DAT_006554fa (0x0065 range — tribe properties)
- DAT_0064b9a0 (0x0064 range — government names)
- DAT_00654fe0/DAT_00654fe4 (0x0065 range — government titles)
- DAT_0064b168 (0x0064 range — commodity names)

**Called by:**
- `004A4249` show_messagebox_4249 [MIXED] — ✗ unreached

**Calls (depth 3):**
```
save_editor_to_rules
└── get_improvement_name [FW]
```

### `00477D8C` load_verify_units

- **Category:** GL | **Size:** 2391 bytes | **Importance:** UI presentation
- **Summary:** The main "load game" UI entry point. Shows file dialog, loads selected save file, verifies unit data integrity, shows title screen if applicable, initializes game state post-load.
- **Mutations:** Writes DAT_006ad6ac (load state flag), DAT_0066ca84 (per-player viewport data), DAT_00655aea (game flags), DAT_006ad2f7 (server flag), DAT_00656108/656106 (unit stack pointers). All in 0x0065-0x006A range — game state.

### `0059B571` netmgr_update_player_list

- **Category:** GL | **Size:** 651 bytes | **Importance:** IMPORTANT — core game logic
- **Summary:** Updates the network player list by inserting/updating a player entry. Removes any existing entry with the same name, then inserts the new entry in alphabetical order by game name. Each entry is a 0x124-byte struct containing player name, game info, and timestamps.
- **Mutations:** YES — modifies linked list in object fields. Player data is in dynamically allocated memory, not in the documented game state ranges.

**Called by:** none (orphan or callback/entry point)

**Calls (depth 3):**

## Diplomacy & Foreign Affairs (18 functions)

### `004C59F0` handle_incident_terror

- **Category:** GL | **Size:** 1465 bytes | **Importance:** IMPORTANT — core game logic
- **Summary:** Handles the diplomatic incident when a spy/diplomat is caught performing espionage. If caught by a human player, offers the choice to declare war. AI automatically responds based on relationship status. May trigger government overthrow scandal if caught by own government's spy.
- **Mutations:** **DAT_0064c6c0** (per-civ flags: 0x10 "spied on" flag set, 0x2000 war declaration), **DAT_0064ca82** (war timestamps via thunk_FUN_00467825)

**Called by:** none (orphan or callback/entry point)

### `00430822` check_diplomacy_timeout

- **Category:** MIXED | **Size:** 140 bytes | **Importance:** IMPORTANT — mixed UI+logic
- **Summary:** Checks if a diplomacy timeout has elapsed. If current_time - last_time >= DAT_006ad8b8 * 60 ticks, or if diplomacy flags are set, it sets a UI flag and invalidates the cache.
- **Mutations:** DAT_006ad678[0xf] |= 0x400 (0x006AXXXX range — game state flag on a unit/map object), DAT_0063f278 = 0 if it was -1 (0x0063 range — UI/diplomacy state)

### `004B81DD` parley_handle_response

- **Category:** MIXED | **Size:** 1177 bytes | **Importance:** UI presentation

### `00511BA2` dispatch_mp_event

- **Category:** MIXED | **Size:** 7252 bytes | **Importance:** IMPORTANT — mixed UI+logic
- **Summary:** Master multiplayer event dispatcher. Dequeues an event from the linked list and dispatches it through a massive switch statement (cases 0x00-0x65, ~102 cases). Handles retirement, barbarian attacks, global warming, space race, city capture, wonder events, diplomacy requests, combat results, espionag
- **Mutations:** - DAT_0064ca82 (treaty status at 0x0064XXXX): Case 0x3d writes treaty values between players
- DAT_0067a8c0 (0x0067XXXX): Modified in case 0x3d (parley request state)
- DAT_0067ab65, DAT_0067ab66 (0x0067XXXX): Set in cases 0x64/0x65 (reveal unit/city info flags)

### `00509B48` city_button_buy

- **Category:** MIXED | **Size:** 1642 bytes | **Importance:** UI presentation
- **Summary:** Handles the "Buy" button in the city window. Calculates rush-buy cost (2x remaining shields for buildings, 2x + shields^2/20 for units, doubled if no production started), shows confirmation, deducts gold, completes production.

### `0040AB41` try_create_inland_sea

- **Category:** GL | **Size:** 281 bytes | **Importance:** IMPORTANT — core game logic
- **Summary:** Attempts to create an inland sea (lake) at the given position. Checks that the tile is valid, not on the map edge, and that all 4 adjacent (2 tiles away) cardinal neighbors are land. If so, sets the tile to ocean (terrain 10). Returns 1 on success, 0 on failure.
- **Mutations:** Writes terrain type to map tile byte 0 via thunk_FUN_005b8931.

### `0059B7FC` netmgr_add_client

- **Summary:** Sets the active AI civ for processing. Validates param_1 is in [0,8], then sets the global active civ index and pointer to that civ's data record.
- **Mutations:** Writes _DAT_0062803c (active civ index, 0x0062xxxx — below game state range) and PTR_DAT_00628040 = &DAT_0064c6a0 + param_1 * 0x594 (pointer into per-civ data).

**Called by:** none (orphan or callback/entry point)

**Calls:** (leaf function)

- **Category:** GL | **Size:** 509 bytes | **Importance:** IMPORTANT — core game logic
- **Summary:** Quickly checks if a save file is valid and loadable. Opens file, reads magic header, checks version, optionally loads game data to verify. Returns error code: 0=success, 1=not a save, 2=old version, 3=read error, 4=new version.

### Classification Summary

| Classification | Count | Notes |
|----------------|-------|-------|
| IMPORTANT — core game logic | 66 | Core GL logic — highest priority for game fidelity |

| UI presentation | 36 | Display/rendering only — no game state impact |
| editor/debug | 22 | Scenario editor or debug — not needed for normal gameplay |
| scenario-only | 1 | Scenario-specific — only for scenario support |

### Likely Explanation for Unreachability

Most of these functions are reachable at runtime through:

1. **Function pointer tables** — dialog callbacks, menu item handlers, button dispatch tables
2. **Conditional paths deeper than depth 8** — long call chains in AI evaluation, combat resolution, etc.
3. **Windows message dispatch** — WndProc and dialog procedures not modeled in static call graph
4. **Scenario event triggers** — events.txt macro execution engine
5. **Multiplayer-only code paths** — activated only in network/hotseat/PBEM sessions
6. **Timer callbacks and idle handlers** — registered via Win32 SetTimer/PostMessage
